<Resp>{'time': 1610152044105, 'text': "MS. JONES, THANK YOU FOR YOUR GREAT REVIEW, I'M GLAD OUR OFFICE ATTENDED TO YOUR DENTAL EMERGENCY. STAY HEALTHY & SAFE."}<//Resp>< Review>
I don't like dentists. I had become accustom to dentists being heavy handed and to me a trip to the dentist that required any procedure meant I was walking out numb but still in pain and hurting for a couple days after. I had to make an emergency appointment. The website gives a number to call in an emergency. I called it and surprisingly it was the actual dentists number. It was pretty early in the morning and I could tell I may have been interrupting his routine. He said he'd call me back after explaining the situation. He called back and gave me an appointment time... Didn't expect that. I get there and due to covid u can't just walk in and they are limiting the number of patients allowed in at a time. In fact they won't let you in more than 10 minutes prior to appointment. I can definitely appreciate the safety measures taken. The asked me the covid questions. Took my temp and handed me hand sanitizer... Within minutes I was x-rayed. Then sat in the chair.The dentist then casually says. I needed a root canal.. Before my mind could fully process and start having anxiety. He was so quick and smooth about everything I didn't even notice the needle he pulled out to numb me. I barely felt it. Normally this is one of the worst parts for me. He told me it'd be quick and he'd have me out of pain in no time. He wasnt lying. He actually paid attention to my reactions and did exactly what he said. I had a root canal and cleaning for the rest of my teeth can honestly say this was the best visit Ive ever had a dentist. I was in and out. Pain relieved. I took ibuprofen that night and the next day and Ive been doing great since. I'm extremely happy with my experience and I will keep him as my dentist. He did a fantastic job.< /Review>

Staff is extremely kind and welcoming every visit.

The chiropractor is funny, kind and listens when you speak. Explains what you need and is friendly if you ask questions about your progress or what you need (always ask questions!).

<text>I've come here for many years.  Go for a walk, watch a pick up soccer game, watch a baseball game, or take your dog to the dog park.  Clean, plenty of free parking and lots of open space.  There are occasional coyotes near the forest as well as a creek.  The creek is shallow and a good place to allow your dog to play.  The path to the creek is near the fenced Soquel Creek Water station. Dogs are required to be on leash outside of the dog park and sometimes the sheriff comes down, but that is pretty rare.
The park is kid friendly though there are no play structures.  Let them run or play sports.  It's all fun.<//text>< user_name>

<rating>5<//rating>< review>
The polo fields have been part of my life since the late 70s. When it was just a field with a walk path around it.  Aptos Creek runs by one side of the park giving my friends and I another playground for teenage boys. Now the Polo Fields is a sports park with baseball fields and enormous grass fields creating multiple soccer fields. A BMX track, a exercise par course with a variety of physical tasks you perform at stations spread out along the walk path that spans the whole park. The Cabrillo Lions Club is very active there . Most of the many benches around the park were donated and installed by this wonderful group of volunteers. It's a perfect use of the land, also a beautiful well maintained park.</review>

Polo Grounds park has several different features: several soccer fields (where a lot of youth soccer games take place), tennis courts, a BMX track with crazy jumps, and a dog run. The main soccer field closest to the entrance has serious terrain problems, but the others are in good shape. The dog run is large and has two separate fenced-in areas, one for big dogs and one for small, each with dog-friendly water fountains and people-friendly chairs.</review>

< Review>
This place has a small service office which gets crowed quickly. The time frame it takes to get work done on your car is usually more than is quoted . Getting through on the phone in the middle of the day takes time. You need to have patients if you take you car here. Hopefully all this has changed and the service department is better, but every time i have visited the place i have had issues. Because of that and the following I only give it 3 stars.
Several years ago I took my Chrysler 300C into their shop for service because my airbag light was on.  The service dept. had issues figuring out why this was happening and had to keep my car several days to do tests.  After paying the bill I got my car back and within a week the light came back on. I returned it to Lithia and this time they said they had to replace a wiring harness in the dash which they tore apart to find the issue. I kept calling for updates and was told a new wiring harness was ordered from the east coast so my car had to sit there until the dash was reassembled. After several days and several more calls to Lithia I found out the harness finally came in but was not the correct one. Lithia ordered a second one which again took a while to arrive. Long story short - (from what I was told from Lithia) the second one was also wrong so they decided to just dig into the dash and rewire the incorrect harness into place onto the correct terminals.
I'm not a mechanic or wiring expert but using something that is incorrect yet making it work doesn't set well with me.
If I recall correctly Lithia had my car over a month to try and repair it. My car was only a few years old at the time. They finally called to say it was ready but then said I needed 4 new tires.  After a month of not having it I believed them because I had forgotten how much tread was actually on the current ones. I'm guessing I could have driven away with my old tires but trusted Lithia for some reason. Those Continental Tires they installed lasted less than 2 years and I had to replace them with something better.
Since then my dash has had a bad rattle in it which drives me nuts eveytime i hit a bump, but do I go back to Lithia to allow them to tear my dash apart again and cause more rattles or just play the radio LOUDER. The loud radio has been my choice so far. I wish I could give a better rating to Lithia but I have not been happy with how things worked out for me and my car. On a side note, my A/C has never worked well since this incident either and I am sure it is directly related to this incident because it worked perfect prior to the wiring harness service Fiasco.
You might be luckier than I. Good luck if you decide to go there for service.</Review>

My 2015 Grand Cherokee is the second Dodge product I've bought from Lithia since early last year.  I bought a 2015 Dodge Ram 1500 last year and it's been the best new vehicle I've bought in many years.  The sale staff and sales strategy at Lithia is why I returned.  No foolish dickering on price while you sit and the salesman and sales manager have coffee in a back office trying to sweat you into paying too much. Bottom line prices are posted right on the windows and you buy or don't buy based on that.  If you ask, they will show you the invoice and if you push a bit you can get a better dealer discount like I did on my Cherokee.

As far as the sales staff, I want to again thank Graham Shillaker.  He is the most knowledgeable sales person I have ever encountered,  If you want to know how something works and want to be shown how all the new technology works he's your man.  I haven't found a question that he doesn't have an immediate answer for.  That is so refreshing these days since other salesmen, at other dealerships generally are so inept they give you the "deer in the headlights" look if you ask and technical or even mechanical questions at all.

I would also like to thank Adam Jones for taking over for Graham to get our paperwork started when Graham had to finish up with other customers he was helping when we returned to make our purchase.

Both of these guys stayed well past quitting time to get our paperwork done and out purchase made.

On the day we purchased the Cherokee, we looked at Acura, Nissan, Ford, Honda and Chevy and none of their products could come close to the quality, workmanship, comfort, performance and features included in the Jeep Grand Cherokee.

One other major factor in our purchase of another Dodge product is the complete satisfaction we have experienced with the Dodge Ram 1500 we bought early last year.  I currently have 13,000 miles on it and it has been the best new truck, so far, I have ever purchased.  Like the Cherokee, it far surpasses the competitors by a long shot in overall quality and workmanship.

<Text>Wolves in sheep's clothing! Buyer Beware!!! I'm not one to write reviews much, or talk bad about anyone or any company, but in this case I cant help but feel the need to warn those who might be fooled by this car dealership. Let me begin with, this is not the first car my wife and I had purchased from a dealership, it is the third. I have nothing but good things to say about the other dealerships I have purchased from. Lithia Chrysler had us fooled, we traded in our beautiful dodge caliber because we needed an AWD or 4 wheel drive vehicle, they showed us a used 2006 Jeep Commander, they were very reluctant to let us view other options, this should have been a warning of how badly they wanted to get rid of this "lemon" It seemed to fit the bill of what we needed so I went ahead and questioned them on everything mechanically about the Jeep, asking about the records and services done. They sold me like a snake oil salesman, informing me that they wouldn't sell anything that wasn't 100% reliable and up to their "high" standards of running and driving. They showed me their evaluation of the car and the things they had done bringing the jeep up to their standards, which included rebuilding the sunroof due to "excess wind noise" They had me convinced it was perfect. Well during the first little rain we had the roof leaked as if the rain clouds themselves had occupied the interior of the car, we had roughly a half inch or water soaking the floorboards, water was literally dripping out of every seam and opening of the the jeep's tan cloth and plastic interior. Come to find out that not one piece of weatherstripping on any door, nor sunroof, nor dual rear passenger moonroofs was any good, ALL OF THEM LEAKED! That hurt my pocket book, but that was simply the beginning! The water damage also hurt the sound system causing the speakers now to sound crackly and underwater, It also harmed the interior roof mounted rear monitor back up display. I had tried and tried contacting the group of men who sold me the faulty vehicle but they stopped returning my phone calls and emails, I lived too far away to simply bring it back for them to look, and worse yet they were not willing to help. Within a couple thousand miles of purchasing the jeep the water pump went out! Again this caused me to open the pocket book when we were in a financially fragile spot. Not long after that the transmission began acting up, the fault being in the AWD/4-wheel drive computer... Soon after the water pump and transmission acting up, the engine itself began having problems due to a faulty TPS "Throttle Position Sensor"
So with a barren pocketbook, we again were forced to act. We have now dumped more money into the Jeep Commander than it is worth. We are belly up, unable to afford a replacement and in more debt because of this car than I care to mention.
